TITLE: Correct Delegate Implementation in NativeScript for iOS
DESCRIPTION: This snippet shows the correct way to implement a delegate for PKPaymentAuthorizationViewController in NativeScript. The delegate is properly retained by assigning it to a variable, preventing premature garbage collection and ensuring expected functionality.

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
let applePayController: PKPaymentAuthorizationViewController
let applePayControllerDelegate: PKPaymentAuthorizationViewControllerDelegateImpl

applePayController =
  PKPaymentAuthorizationViewController.alloc().initWithPaymentRequest(
    paymentRequest,
  )
applePayControllerDelegate =
  PKPaymentAuthorizationViewControllerDelegateImpl.initWithOwner(this)
applePayController.delegate = applePayControllerDelegate

TITLE: Defining Frontmatter in Markdown for NativeScript Docs
DESCRIPTION: This snippet demonstrates how to set frontmatter options for a NativeScript documentation page, including title, description, category, navigation links, and contributors.

LANGUAGE: markdown
CODE:
---
title: Some title
description: the page description, shown below the title and set in the description meta tags
category: the name/text of the page category, show in the breadcrumbs and above the title
categoryLink: the link where the custom category should link to
prev: the URL where the `Previous` button at the bottom should link to
prevText: the text to show in the `Previous` button. By default the text is looked up in the sidebar.
next: the URL where the `Next` button at the bottom should link to
nextText: the text to show in the `Next` button. By default the text is looked up in the sidebar.
contributors: false # to disable the contributors list in the right sidebar
contributors:
 - GitHubUsername1
 - GitHubUsername2
---

    tintColor="green"

  />

    src="sys://photo.on.rectangle.angled"
    tintColor="green"

    row="1"
    src="sys://photo.on.rectangle.angled"
    tintColor="green"

    row="1"

    src="sys://photo.on.rectangle.angled"

TITLE: Creating Details Page in NativeScript
DESCRIPTION: Implements the details page component, including the view model and XML layout for displaying movie details.

LANGUAGE: javascript
CODE:
// app/details/details-page.js

import { DetailsViewModel } from './details-view-model'

export function navigatingTo(args) {
  const page = args.object
  page.bindingContext = new DetailsViewModel(page.navigationContext)
}

LANGUAGE: javascript
CODE:
// app/details/details-view-model.js

import { Observable } from '@nativescript/core'
import { FlickService } from '../services/flick.service'

export class DetailsViewModel extends Observable {
  #flick

  constructor(_context) {
    super()
    this.#flick = FlickService.getInstance().getFlickById(_context.flickId)
  }

  get flick() {
    return this.#flick
  }
}

LANGUAGE: xml
CODE:
<!-- app/details/details-page.xml -->
<Page xmlns="http://schemas.nativescript.org/tns.xsd" navigatingTo="navigatingTo">
  <ActionBar title="{{ flick.title }}" />
  <ScrollView>
    <StackLayout>
      <Image margin="10" stretch="aspectFill" src="{{ flick.image }}" />
      <StackLayout padding="10 20">
        <Repeater items="{{ flick.details }}">
          <Repeater.itemTemplate>
            <StackLayout>
              <Label marginTop="15" fontSize="16" fontWeight="700" class="text-primary" textWrap="true" text="{{ $value.title }}" />
              <Label fontSize="14" class="text-secondary" textWrap="true" text="{{ $value.body }}" />
            </StackLayout>
          </Repeater.itemTemplate>
        </Repeater>
      </StackLayout>
    </StackLayout>
  </ScrollView>
</Page>

TITLE: Implementing HtmlView in NativeScript React

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
import * as React from 'react'
import { HtmlView } from '@nativescript/core'

export function HtmlViewExample() {
  const htmlString = '<h1>HtmlView</h1><p>This is an example of using HtmlView</p>'

  const onHtmlViewLoaded = (args) => {
    console.log(`HtmlView loaded`)
  }

  return (
    <HtmlView
      html={htmlString}
      onLoaded={onHtmlViewLoaded}
    />
  )
}

  totalAmount: string
  message: string
  deliveryTime: number
}

  static updateActivity(
    data: Pick<AppleWidgetModelData, 'message' | 'deliveryTime'>,
  ): void
  static cancelActivity(data: Pick<AppleWidgetModelData, 'message'>): void
  static updateWidget(): void
  static updateDataWithKey(key: string, data: string): void
  static getDataWithKey(key: string): string
  static removeDataWithKey(key: string): void
}

TITLE: Defining AndroidActivityCallbacks Interface in TypeScript
DESCRIPTION: This code snippet defines the AndroidActivityCallbacks interface, which includes methods for handling Android activity lifecycle events, user interactions, and permissions. It provides a bridge between NativeScript and Android native functionality.

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
interface AndroidActivityCallbacks {
  getRootView(): View;
  onActivityResult(
  activity: any,
  requestCode: number,
  resultCode: number,
  data: any,
  superFunc: Function
): any;
  onBackPressed(activity: any, superFunc: Function): void;
  onCreate(
  activity: any,
  savedInstanceState: any,
  intent: any,
  superFunc: Function
): void;
  onDestroy(activity: any, superFunc: Function): void;
  onNewIntent(
  activity: any,
  intent: any,
  superSetIntentFunc: Function,
  superFunc: Function
): void;
  onPostResume(activity: any, superFunc: Function): void;
  onRequestPermissionsResult(
  activity: any,
  requestCode: number,
  permissions: string[],
  grantResults: number[],
  superFunc: Function
): void;
  onSaveInstanceState(activity: any, outState: any, superFunc: Function): void;
  onStart(activity: any, superFunc: Function): void;
  onStop(activity: any, superFunc: Function): void;
  resetActivityContent(activity: any): void;
}

TITLE: Component Scoped CSS
DESCRIPTION: Demonstrates proper CSS scoping for custom components to prevent style leakage

LANGUAGE: xml
CODE:
<StackLayout class="my-component">
  <Label text="Custom component layout" class="label" />
</StackLayout>

LANGUAGE: css
CODE:
/* GOOD: This will ONLY apply to the custom component */
.my-component .label {
  color: blue;
}

/* BAD: This will apply to the custom component AND potentially to the page where the component is used */
.label {
  color: blue;
}

TITLE: Initializing and Registering Themes in NativeScript
DESCRIPTION: Example of how to use the initThemes() function to register multiple themes in a NativeScript application. This should be called in the app's entry point before the app starts.

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
import { initThemes, switchTheme } from '@nativescript/theme-switcher'

// first initialize the themes
initThemes({
  // default is optional - will be auto-applied after initializing (*)
  default: () => import('theme-loader!./themes/default.scss'),
  red: () => import('theme-loader!./themes/red.scss'),
  green: () => import('theme-loader!./themes/green.scss'),
})

  {

TITLE: Setting up Sidebar Navigation with Vue and TypeScript
DESCRIPTION: This snippet sets up the sidebar navigation for the Core Reference documentation using Vue 3 and TypeScript. It imports a sidebar configuration and defines a function to filter sidebar items by category.

LANGUAGE: vue
CODE:
<script setup lang="ts">
  import uiSidebar from "./sidebar";

  function category(name: string) {
    return uiSidebar[0].items.find(i => i.text === name).items
  }
</script>

TITLE: Setting and Cleaning Up setInterval in NativeScript TypeScript
DESCRIPTION: This snippet shows how to set an interval and properly clean it up to prevent resource consumption. It sets an interval and stores the reference, then provides a cleanup method to clear the interval if it exists.

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
this.myInterval = setInterval(() => {
  // something
}, 2000);

cleanup() {
  if (typeof this.myInterval === 'number') {
    clearInterval(this.myInterval);
    this.myInterval = null;
  }
}

TITLE: Implementing Navigation in NativeScript Svelte App
DESCRIPTION: Adds navigation functionality to the home page, allowing users to tap on a flick item to navigate to its details page. It uses the 'navigate' function from svelte-native.

LANGUAGE: XML
CODE:
<page>
  <actionBar title="NativeFlix" />
  <stackLayout height="100%">
    <listView
      height="100%"
      separatorColor="transparent"
      items="{flicks}"
      on:itemTap="{onFlickTap}"
    >
      <!-- ListView content -->
    </listView>
  </stackLayout>
</page>

<script>
  import { navigate } from 'svelte-native'
  import { Template } from 'svelte-native/components'
  import { FlickService } from '../services/FlickService'
  import Details from './Details.svelte'

  let flicks = FlickService.getInstance().getFlicks()

  function onFlickTap(event) {
    navigate({
      page: Details,
      props: { flickId: flicks[event.index].id }
    })
  }
</script>

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Inefficient ListView Setup with Conditional Rendering in NativeScript XML
DESCRIPTION: This snippet demonstrates a poor implementation of a ListView using conditional rendering, which can cause performance issues due to creation and destruction of view elements during scrolling.

LANGUAGE: xml
CODE:
<ListView items="{{ myTitles }}" class="list-group">
  <ListView.itemTemplate>
    <StackLayout>
      <r:Render when="{{ !showSomethingElse }}">
        <r:Render.template>
          <StackLayout backgroundColor="lightblue">
            <Label text="{{ title }}" textWrap="true" class="title" />
          </StackLayout>
        </r:Render.template>
      </r:Render>
      <r:Render when="{{ showSomethingElse }}">
        <r:Render.template>
          <GridLayout rows="auto,5,auto,5,auto" backgroundColor="red">
            <Label text="{{ title }}" textWrap="true" class="title" />
            <Label row="2" text="Something Else" textWrap="true" class="title" />
            <Label
              row="4"
              text="Could show yet anything thing here"
              textWrap="true"
              class="title"
            />
          </GridLayout>
        </r:Render.template>
      </r:Render>
    </StackLayout>
  </ListView.itemTemplate>
</ListView>

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
import {
  registerJetpackCompose,
  ComposeDataDriver,
} from '@nativescript/jetpack-compose'

// A. You can generate types for your own Compose Provider with 'ns typings android --aar {path/to/{name}.aar}'
// B. Otherwise you can ignore by declaring the package resolution path you know you provided
declare var com
registerJetpackCompose(
  'flyingHearts',
  (view) => new ComposeDataDriver(new com.example.FlyingHearts(), view),
)

TITLE: XCode Development Team Configuration
DESCRIPTION: Ruby script for Podfile to set development team ID or disable code signing for all targets in XCode project.

LANGUAGE: ruby
CODE:
post_install do |installer|
  installer.pods_project.targets.each do |target|
    target.build_configurations.each do |config|
      # either set the DEVELOPMENT_TEAM explicitly
      config.build_settings['DEVELOPMENT_TEAM'] = '<TEAM_ID>'
      # or disable code signing
      config.build_settings['CODE_SIGNING_ALLOWED'] = 'NO'
    end
  end
end

}

  animation-name: example;
  animation-duration: 4s;
  animation-fill-mode: forwards;
}

.ns-light {
  .bg-primary {
    background-color: #fdfdfd;
  }
  .bg-secondary {
    background-color: #ffffff;
  }
  .text-primary {
    color: #444;
  }
  .text-secondary {
    color: #777;
  }
}

.ns-dark {
  .bg-primary {
    background-color: #212121;
  }
  .bg-secondary {
    background-color: #383838;
  }
  .text-primary {
    color: #eee;
  }
  .text-secondary {
    color: #ccc;
  }
}

TITLE: Creating a Data Service in NativeScript
DESCRIPTION: Implements a FlickService class to manage and provide access to movie data within the application.

LANGUAGE: javascript
CODE:
// app/services/flick.service.js
export class FlickService {
  #flicks = [
    {
      id: 1,
      genre: 'Musical',
      title: 'Book of Mormon',
      image: '~/assets/bookofmormon.png',
      url: 'https://nativescript.org/images/ngconf/book-of-mormon.mov',
      description: `A satirical examination of the beliefs and practices of The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints.`,
      details: [
        {
          title: 'Music, Lyrics and Book by',
          body: 'Trey Parker, Robert Lopez, and Matt Stone',
        },
        // ... more details
      ],
    },
    // ... more flicks
  ]

  static getInstance() {
    return FlickService.#instance
  }

  static #instance = new FlickService()

  getFlicks() {
    return this.#flicks
  }

  getFlickById(id) {
    return this.#flicks.find((flick) => flick.id === id) || undefined
  }
}

----------------------------------------

TITLE: Implementing DetailsComponent logic in Angular
DESCRIPTION: Implements the TypeScript logic for the DetailsComponent, including route parameter handling and data retrieval.

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
@Component({
  moduleId: module.id,
  selector: 'ns-details',
  templateUrl: 'details.component.html'
})
export class DetailsComponent {
  flick: FlickModel | undefined = undefined

  constructor(
    private activatedRoute: ActivatedRoute,
    private flickService: FlickService
  ) {}

  ngOnInit(): void {
    const id = +this.activatedRoute.snapshot.params.id
    if (id) {
      this.flick = this.flickService.getFlickById(id)
    }
  }
}

    <GridLayout
      height="280"
      rows="*, auto, auto"
      columns="*"
      class="bg-secondary"
      borderRadius="10"
      margin="5 10"
      padding="0"
    >
      <Image row="0" margin="0" stretch="aspectFill" [src]="item.image"></Image>
      <Label
        row="1"
        margin="10 10 0 10"
        fontWeight="700"
        class="text-primary"
        fontSize="18"

      ></Label>
      <Label
        row="2"
        margin="0 10 10 10"
        class="text-secondary"

        textWrap="true"

      ></Label>

  </ng-template>
</ListView>

TITLE: Inefficient Method-Based View Binding in NativeScript
DESCRIPTION: Example demonstrating poor practice of using method bindings in NativeScript views. This approach causes unnecessary binding execution and degrades view rendering performance.

LANGUAGE: xml
CODE:
// view markup
<Label text="{{getMyText}} />

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
// view binding class
export class ViewBinding extends Observable {
  getMyText() {
    return 'label text'
  }
}

TITLE: Defining TouchGestureEventData Interface in TypeScript
DESCRIPTION: TypeScript interface definition for touch gesture event data. Extends TapGestureEventData and provides properties and methods for handling touch interactions including action states and pointer management.

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
interface TouchGestureEventData extends TapGestureEventData {
  action: "up" | "move" | "down" | "cancel";
  getActivePointers(): Pointer[];
  getAllPointers(): Pointer[];
}

interface PropertyChangeData extends EventData {

TITLE: NavigationEntry Interface Definition in TypeScript
DESCRIPTION: Defines the NavigationEntry interface that extends ViewEntry and contains properties for controlling navigation behavior including animations, history, context, and platform-specific transitions.

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
interface NavigationEntry extends ViewEntry {
  animated: boolean;
  backstackVisible: boolean;
  bindingContext: any;
  clearHistory: boolean;
  context: any;
  transition: NavigationTransition;
  transitionAndroid: NavigationTransition;
  transitioniOS: NavigationTransition;
}

TITLE: Defining DownloadRequest Interface in TypeScript for NativeScript
DESCRIPTION: This code snippet defines the DownloadRequest interface, which represents a single download request in NativeScript. It includes properties for the download URL and key, as well as callback functions for handling completion and errors.

LANGUAGE: TypeScript
CODE:
interface DownloadRequest {
  completed: (image: any, key: string) => void;
  error: (key: string) => void;
  key: string;
  url: string;
}

DESCRIPTION: Declares the BackstackEntry interface with two properties: entry of type NavigationEntry and resolvedPage of type Page. This interface represents an entry in the back stack of a Frame object in NativeScript applications.

LANGUAGE: typescript
CODE:
interface BackstackEntry {
  entry: NavigationEntry;
  resolvedPage: Page;
}
